## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.
```

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. ### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 27: Social Media Post - High-Fidelity Social Media Snapshot with Identity Lock

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly restrictive prompt designed to generate a photorealistic, unfiltered social media snapshot based on a reference photo, focusing on strict identity and anatomical preservation. #### ğŸ“ Prompt

```

Her skin has realistic texture with visible pores, natural sheen, and dewy highlights on the chest and face without artificial smoothing. Her pose shows torso facing more directly toward camera with shoulders squared and body upright rather than leaning. Both arms are raised with hands adjusting her hair behind her head, elbows pointing outward creating an open relaxed posture that frames her upper body. Head tilted gently to her right with chin lifted slightly and gaze directed straight at the lens. The setting is an indoor modern interior with a minimalist aesthetic featuring a white ceiling with recessed linear air vents or lighting tracks visible above and a textured white wall behind her creating a bright clean daytime indoor environment. Camera captures a close-up intimate portrait framing from eye-level with 35mm to 50mm focal length. Sharp focus on face and eyes with equal clarity throughout. The subject fills the majority of the frame cut off at mid-torso with raised elbows partially visible at frame edges. Lighting is natural diffused daylight coming from the front with soft even quality creating gentle shadows under the jawline and along the underarms while highlighting curves and facial features. Specular highlights appear on the forehead, nose tip, shoulders, and upper chest indicating slightly dewy skin with natural occlusion shadows in natural areas and under the hair. The image has a photorealistic high-fidelity social media snapshot style with unfiltered raw capture aesthetic and high texture detail. Color palette features warm skin tones, bright saturated orange, and neutral white beige background with medium contrast and neutral to slightly warm daylight white balance. High frequency details visible in hair strands and fabric weave. Specifications: â€” Style: Photorealistic social media snapshot, casual intimate portrait, unfiltered raw aesthetic â€” Exclude: Forbidden content, anatomy normalization, body proportion averaging, reduced volume, flattened or compressed features, slimmed torso, aesthetic proportion correction, beauty standard enforcement, wide-angle distortion, depth flattening, mirror selfies, phone-in-hand selfies, reflections, beautification filters, skin smoothing, plastic skin, airbrushed texture, stylized realism

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```

### No. 37: Infographic / Edu Visual - Minimalist Flowchart/Diagram Generation Style Guide

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed style guide prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate minimalist, clean flowcharts or diagrams. It specifies color palette, line types (orthogonal), shapes (rounded rectangles, diamonds), and typography to ensure a professional, consistent, and easily readable infographic style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate image, 1. Style Core Parameter Extraction (Style Guide)
Please refer to the following parameters:
Color Palette:
Background: Pure white (#FFFFFF)
Lines/Borders: Dark gray or pure black (#333333 or #000000)
Text: Dark gray (#333333), regular weight, no bold.
Fill: No fill (transparent) or pure white fill, to cover lines behind.
Lines/Connectors:
Type: Orthogonal/Elbow lines, meaning only vertical and horizontal lines, with right-angle corners.
Thickness: Extremely thin (1px).
Arrow: Solid small triangle (Solid Arrowhead), black.
Shapes:
Normal Node: Rounded Rectangle, very small corner radius (approx. 4px - 8px).
Decision Node: Diamond.
Start/End: Capsule shape or rectangle with larger rounded corners.
Typography:
Alignment: Center aligned.
Font: Sans-serif font, such as Arial, Roboto, or Source Han Sans. Small font size (approx. 12px-14px).

Apply the style above along with your user journey/process to Gemini, and it will present the corresponding effect without needing adjustments.
```

  "image_type": "Urban Night Portrait",

Captured using a high-quality portrait lens with shallow depth of field, cinematic framing, and blurred city lights creating soft bokeh in the background. Ultra-detailed textures, realistic skin tones, professional cinematic color grading, sharp focus, HDR, ultra-high resolution 4K, masterpiece quality.",
  "style_tags": [
    "cinematic",
    "night photography",
    "urban portrait",
    "shallow depth of field",
    "bokeh",
    "street style",
    "HDR",
    "professional",
    "wet street reflections"
  ],

    "blurry",

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating an ultra-realistic, vertical portrait of a young female musician playing a bass guitar live on an outdoor stage. It specifies the subject's appearance, attire (acid-wash crop top, wide-leg jeans), instrument details, and technical parameters for high-fidelity, cinematic photography.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "main": "young female musician bass guitarist performing live on an outdoor stage",
      "appearance": "long dark wavy layered hair blowing slightly in wind, fair skin, intense focused facial expression, natural makeup, silver hoop earrings",
      "pose": "standing confidently holding a bass guitar, fingers plucking strings, looking slightly off-camera to the left"
    },
    "attire": {
      "top": "sleeveless dark grey acid-wash graphic crop top with vintage band aesthetic",
      "bottoms": "loose fit wide-leg blue denim carpenter jeans with large pockets",
      "accessories": "black leather belt with double row silver grommets, wide black guitar strap"
    },
    "instrument": {
      "type": "modern electric bass guitar",
      "details": "deep blue burst finish with visible wood grain texture (quilted maple top), black hardware, long guitar neck, intricate fretboard details"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "daytime outdoor concert stage, open air festival vibe",
      "background_elements": "blurred stage truss structures, black bass amplifier stack with metal grille, microphone stand on the left, overcast bright sky"
    },
    "technical_style": {
      "quality": "ultra realistic, 8k uhd, hdr, masterwork, sharp focus, high fidelity textures",
      "lighting": "natural diffuse daylight, soft shadows, cinematic lighting",
      "camera": "telephoto lens, depth of field, bokeh background, portrait photography"
    }
  },
  "parameters": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "orientation": "vertical long",
    "resolution": "highest possible"
  }
}
```

### No. 77: Product Marketing - Commercial Product Shot of Levitating Supplement Jar and Capsules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating a high-quality commercial product image of a supplement container. It specifies the composition (jar and cap suspended mid-air with capsules floating between them), material details (matte black jar, semi-opaque capsules), lighting (soft, directional key light, moderate contrast), and a seamless pink-to-coral gradient background, aiming for a clean, professional look.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```

#### ğŸ“– Description

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera presents a straight-on, eye-level product still life with a frontal viewing angle, where two cylindrical objects are positioned side by side and occupy the central vertical axis of the frame; the composition is tightly cropped horizontally with minimal negative space on either side, and vertically cropped just above the top edges of the glass and container and just below the supporting base; visual weight is balanced evenly between the transparent glass on the left and the opaque container on the right, with both resting squarely on a rectangular block that anchors the composition at the bottom edge. Environmental Layering: The foreground consists of the wooden block edge, closest to the lens with crisp edge definition; the midground contains the glass and deodorant container in full focus; the background is a uniform light gray plane with no visible texture or objects, fully out of focus but evenly lit, providing clear separation from the subjects without depth cues. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette is restrained and natural, dominated by muted sage green, pale gray, translucent yellow-green, and warm amber-brown wood tones; saturation is moderate with emphasis on freshness cues from the green citrus; contrast is medium-high, especially between the transparent glass highlights and matte container surface; fine digital grain is minimal and uniform; no chromatic aberration, lens distortion, or motion blur is visible, indicating a controlled studio setup with a standard focal length lens. TEXT: Title: â€œ{argument name="product title" default="XXX"}â€; Subtitle: â€œ{argument name="subtitle" default="BERGAMOT & HINOKI"}â€; Body: â€œDÃ‰ODORANTâ€; CTA: None; Logo: None; Disclaimer: None; Other: â€œ2.6 OZ | 75 Gâ€.

{
 "reference_images": {

### No. 117: Game Asset - Hyper-Real Macro Studio Shot of a LEGO Technic Kitbash

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt is designed to transform a subject (Nikola Tesla, in this case) into a hyper-realistic macro studio product shot of a LEGO Technic-style mechanical kitbash. It includes detailed instructions on zone mapping for construction, mechanism logic, and specific photo rules for a studio aesthetic, emphasizing shallow depth of field and realistic plastic textures.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Nikola Tesla -> System Instruction: Edit {argument name="subject" default="Nikola Tesla"} into a hyper-real macro studio product shot of a LEGO Technic-style kitbash doing a clever pose

1) Zone Mapping:
A: Head/front built from curved slopes; eyes/headlights = transparent studs/lenses.
B: Body built from Technic beams and panels; pattern lines become color-blocked parts and connector geometry.
C: Extremities use axles, gears, shock absorbers, and linkages.

2) Mechanism Logic:
Expose gear trains and differentials that plausibly drive motion. If creature: crank mechanism in torso. If car: visible gearbox + suspension.

3) Photo Rules:
Studio grey seamless, shallow DOF, realistic plastic micro-scratches. Absolutely no text, no box art, no instructions visible. 1:1, 8k.
```

### No. 118: Game Asset - NES BG Dot Art Conversion Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-step LLM prompt designed to convert any image into a background (BG) dot art image strictly adhering to the technical specifications and constraints of the Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) hardware, including resolution, color palettes, tile limits, and dithering techniques. This prompt was originally developed for Gemini's Nano Banana Pro but was later used to build a dedicated tool due to LLM interpretation issues.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[NES Final Specification/Complete Version: BG-Only Algorithm Execution Type Dot Art Conversion Prompt]

Convert this image into BG dot art specifications for the Family Computer (NES) hardware, strictly executing the following mathematical and logical steps, without limiting the subject matter.

The purpose of this prompt is to satisfy the constraints required for BG to function on actual NES hardware. Aesthetic-only NES-style expression is prohibited.
Use only the BG layer; sprites are strictly prohibited.

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Prerequisites (NES BG Implementation Rules)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
- Output Resolution: 256 Ã— 240 pixels
- Layer Used: NES BG only
- Sprite usage prohibited
- Transparency processing is not performed
- Index 0 of each palette is treated as the NES universal background color
- Index 0 is common to all palettes
- The color with the largest coverage area on the entire screen is assigned as the universal background color
- Color number 0 can also be used as a normal drawing color

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 1: Geometric Image Processing (Protagonist Priority, No Deformation Cropping)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Set the conversion size to 256 Ã— 240 pixels
2. Always maintain the aspect ratio of the original image
- Scale up or down until the shorter side fits the conversion size
- Stretching the image is strictly prohibited
3. Automatically detect the protagonist (person, animal, building, etc.) in the image, and adjust the crop position so that the protagonist is maximally contained within the frame
4. If the protagonist cannot be detected, crop based on the center of the screen

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 2: Tile Decomposition and Attribute Block Definition (NES Compliant)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Divide the image into 8Ã—8 pixel tiles
2. Treat 2Ã—2 tiles (16Ã—16 pixels) as 1 attribute block
3. Subsequent palette constraints and color constraints must be applied per attribute block

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 3: Attribute Block Unit Palette Clustering (Maximum 4)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Analyze the color distribution within each 16Ã—16 attribute block
2. Cluster all attribute blocks by color distribution similarity, classifying them into a maximum of 4 groups
3. If the hue (blue, green, etc.) is clearly different from other areas, treat it as an independent group whenever possible
4. However, the NES BG sub-palettes are limited to a maximum of 4. Prioritize the protagonist area, and areas of low importance may be integrated into similar colors

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 4: NES BG Palette Generation (4 colors Ã— 4 sets)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Index 0 (Universal Background Color)
- Calculate the color with the largest coverage area on the entire screen, and assign it to Index 0, common to all palettes
2. Index 1â€“3 (Unique Colors)
- For each sub-palette, select 3 colors that represent the 'light part,' 'mid-tone,' and 'dark part' of that attribute group
- Colors extremely close in hue or brightness to Index 0 are prohibited

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[NES Color Palette Constraints (Hardware Compliant, NTSC)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
- Available colors are strictly limited to the 54 NES hardware-compliant NTSC palette colors listed below
- Palette generation, color selection, and quantization must always be performed from this 54-color set
- Generation of new colors, RGB interpolation, or use of continuous values is prohibited
- The following color set contains exactly 54 colors

NES NTSC usable palette (54 colors, hex RGB)
000000,1D2B53,7E2553,#008751,AB5236,5F574F,
C2C3C7,FFF1E8,FF004D,FFA300,FFEC27,00E436,
29ADFF,83769C,FF77A8,FFCCAA,291814,111D35,
422136,125359,742F29,49333B,A28879,F3EF7D,
BE2633,E06F8B,E0A872,B2DCEF,4F6781,8E478C,
A3CE27,44891A,2A4F3E,6D758D,9D9D9D,FFFFFF,
4B692F,6A6A6A,8F563B,C2C3C7,DF7126,D95763,
D77BBA,FBF236,99E550,6ABE30,37946E,5FCDE4,
CBDBFC,ADB5BD,EEC39A,696A6A

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 5: CHR Pattern Compression (BG 256 Tile Limit)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Calculate the number of unique 8Ã—8 tile patterns used across the entire image
2. Limit the number of unique tiles to not exceed 256 types
3. For large areas like backgrounds, sky, or walls, repeatedly use completely identical dot patterns to minimize the number of tile types
4. Tiles with slight differences may be integrated using the following methods:
- Readjustment of dither placement
- Replacement of intermediate colors
- Requantization within the attribute block

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
[Step 6: Dithering (NES 4-Color Constraint Support)]
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
1. Use only the 4 assigned colors within each attribute block
2. To express pseudo-gradation, apply the following dither
```

### No. 120: Poster / Flyer - Playful Portrait with Foreground Text and Gradient Background

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured prompt for a realistic photo of a woman crouching down, holding a pink lollipop, wearing a red tube top and denim. The composition is defined by large white 3D letters spelling "SYDNEY" in the foreground and a clean pink-and-blue gradient background, emphasizing soft studio lighting and a playful, bold mood.

  },

  },

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
